    <article class="markdown-body entry-content" itemprop="text"><p><span id="user-content-disable_router_nav_history_direction_check"></span></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-the-nobel-whitepaper" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-nobel-whitepaper"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>The NOBEL Whitepaper</h1>
<p>written by Achim Mertens</p>
<p>The purpose of the NOBEL-token is to honour the people that Alfred Nobel would appreciate. People, that do good things to other people, should be rewarded with this coin. The NOBEL is an high effective charity distribution tool, where the donators either support their favorite beneficence helpers directly or leave it up to the community to care about, that the money goes to the right places. The beneficence helpers do âProof of Charityâ by writing blogs about their work. <a href="https://steemit.com/" rel="nofollow">STEEM</a>Â (the base of NOBEL) is a great blockchain platform with a big and good minded community, that creates value by connecting the right people. No NGO or middleman is needed.</p>
<p><a href="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/alfred_nobel-1.png" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fd0f6993f248339d40c3dd217f563e04e1edec42/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30372f616c667265645f6e6f62656c2d312e706e67" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/alfred_nobel-1.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Â  Â <br>
<em>(Sketch of Alfred Nobel by Achim Mertens)</em></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-content" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Content:</h1>
<ul>
<li>The Problem</li>
<li>The Solution</li>
<li>Six Winning Participants With NOBEL</li>
<li>Some Rules</li>
<li>The Whales</li>
<li>NOBEL FAQ</li>
<li>Further Information About NOBEL</li>
<li>Disclaimer</li>
<li>Contact</li>
<li>Steem FAQ</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-the-problem" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-problem"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>The Problem:</h1>
<p>A lot of people in the world work on charity projects or help their neighbors or do other good things to people. They donât get rewarded for this and therefore they cannot help effectively nor do they have money for themselves (and need to have another job). On the other hand there are people willing to support people in need, but they don't know how to hand over the money to them. With NGOs the donators don't see really what happens with their money. Also there is a loss due to transaction costs and middlemen. This is the targetgroup for the NOBEL world:</p>
<ul>
<li>People, who need help.</li>
<li>People, who want to do something that counts to someone.</li>
<li>Donators, that don't want to spent 20% of their money to administration.</li>
<li>Donators, that want to gift directly to needy people.</li>
<li>Donators, that want to leave the decision, who shell get the money, to a trustworthy selfcontrolling community.</li>
<li>Donators, that want to see concrete results.</li>
<li>Curators, that want to upvote good content to bring the donated money to the right places.</li>
<li>Charity helpers, that want to get publicity and/or support.</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/09/nobel_community.jpg" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/d1f205065ab1ed95f9cb33d04c8b42c6070bf778/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30392f6e6f62656c5f636f6d6d756e6974792e6a7067" alt="Nobel Community" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/09/nobel_community.jpg" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â </p>
<h1><a id="user-content-the-solution" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-solution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>The Solution:</h1>
<p>With the NOBEL coin everyone can help to support the supporters. Everyone who has a STEEM-account (you can register <a href="https://steemit.com" rel="nofollow">here</a>) can buy NOBEL coins on <a href="https://steem-engine.com" rel="nofollow">Steem-Engine-com</a>. That money stabilizes the price. The coin can then be gifted to people working on charity projects or can be staked and the upvote-power can be used to support the charity helpers. <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9b5b81a65257b07859ecb08d08ade56c013a59ba/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30392f6e6f62656c5f343070782e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9b5b81a65257b07859ecb08d08ade56c013a59ba/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30392f6e6f62656c5f343070782e706e67" alt="Nobel_40px" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/09/nobel_40px.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-approach" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#approach"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Approach:</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<ul>
<li>NOBEL offers a blockchain based donating system, that eliminates the middlemen.</li>
<li>NOBEL offers a good hearded community, that brings together charity givers and takers.</li>
<li>NOBEL offers a sense in this chaotic world and the feeling to be important.</li>
<li>The main goal with the NOBEL token is to appreciate humanity.</li>
<li>The actors (more details see below "6 winning participants"):
<ul>
<li>A donator
<ul>
<li>can buy NOBEL. This money backs the system.</li>
<li>can use the NOBEL to donate them directly to charity helpers.</li>
<li>can stake the NOBEL and with that she can curate good Proof of Charity.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>An Investor
<ul>
<li>can buy NOBEL token and wait until it raises in value.</li>
<li>knows, that his money is placed in a good humanitarian environment.</li>
<li>owns parts of the NOBEL system. The coins are also shares.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A charity helper
<ul>
<li>gets support and thanks for his work.</li>
<li>needs to write good posts about his work (Proof of Charity).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A curator
<ul>
<li>should get some NOBEL token and stake them. This gives her higher weighted voting power.</li>
<li>With her upvotes she gives posts with hashtag #nobel a value, that is appreciated by the Scotbot.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The Scotbot
<ul>
<li>This bot has a lot of NOBEL token in his backpack.</li>
<li>The bot checks each post on the STEEM blockchain, that is tagged with #nobel.</li>
<li>The bot gives the author and the curators a small amount of NOBEL, depending on the number and power of upvotes.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The needy people
<ul>
<li>They just receive attention and a bit hope.</li>
<li>They should be willing to get out of their situation.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The NOBEL token is an automated system, based on the STEEM blockchain, that warranties, that all these actors find together and that their interactions are fullfilled trustworthy.</li>
<li>There have been 1,000,000,000 (10 ^ 9) NOBEL coins created initially on July 19. 2019 by Achim Mertens.</li>
<li>The authors, curators and the token creator earn STEEM also with each post they write or curate. This is their salary. They can also sell the NOBEL token, but at least for the whales this should not be the first option to keep the price high and trust into that system.</li>
<li>The frontend is <a href="http://nobel.charity" rel="nofollow">http://nobel.charity</a>. This has the look and feel like other social medias, except that there is a "price" for each post, that shows the value of NOBEL. Other Steem-frontends like steemit.com or steempeak.com or busy.org do also work, then you need some filters to find the NOBEL community (i.e. .../created/nobel).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-benefits" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#benefits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Â Benefits:</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Value for the participants:</p>
<ul>
<li>The NOBEL-System was created to be self-amplifying. The more people join, the more stable gets the system.</li>
<li>The owner of NOBEL tokens are the owner of this system. With their voting power they can influence the next steps.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Measurements:</p>
<ul>
<li>There are some tools to see what is going on:
<ul>
<li><a href="https://nobel.charity" rel="nofollow">https://nobel.charity</a> (or <a href="https://steemit.com/created/nobel" rel="nofollow">https://steemit.com/created/nobel</a>)
<ul>
<li>This page is the basic entry to the system. There one can see all posts with the hashtag #nobel. It is based on the STEEM platform. To join you need a STEEM account.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="https://steem-engine.com/?p=sign_in" rel="nofollow">https://steem-engine.com/?p=sign_in</a>
<ul>
<li>Here you can exchange STEEM into NOBEL and backwards. You can claim your NOBEL tokens there.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="https://steem-engine.rocks/transactions?symbol=nobel" rel="nofollow">https://steem-engine.rocks/transactions?symbol=nobel</a>
<ul>
<li>Here you can see who and how many people are transacting NOBEL. Also you can observe the Scotbot and check out, if it does what it should do.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=curation_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100" rel="nofollow">http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=curation_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100</a> Or <a href="http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=curation_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100&amp;author=ireneblessing" rel="nofollow">http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=curation_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100&amp;author=ireneblessing</a>
<ul>
<li>Here you can see what a curator (in this example @ireneblessing) has earned.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=author_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100" rel="nofollow">http://scot-api.steem-engine.com/get_account_history?account=achimmertens&amp;type=author_reward&amp;token=NOBEL&amp;limit=100</a>
<ul>
<li>Here you can see what an author has earned (in this example @achimmertens).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Monetizing:</p>
<ul>
<li>When you have a STEEM account, you can see the total of all STEEM and subcoins like NOBEL in your wallet. This amount is shown in your local currency, depending on the current market value. You can send STEEM to a crypto exchange and there you can receive the money in your local currency.
<ul>
<li>Example of the wallet from @achimmertens: <a href="https://steempeak.com/@achimmertens/transfers" rel="nofollow">https://steempeak.com/@achimmertens/transfers</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-competition" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#competition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Competition:</h2>
<ul>
<li>Proof of Charity via blockchain is a very new topic. As far as I know is the NOBEL token in this form unique. There are some similar systems like:
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.binance.com/de" rel="nofollow">https://www.binance.com/de</a> -&gt; They have charity projects, based on blockchain.</li>
<li><a href="https://community.coinsence.org/dashboard" rel="nofollow">https://community.coinsence.org/dashboard</a> -&gt; They have small working groups with own currencies (partly via blockchain)</li>
<li><a href="https://Fundition.io" rel="nofollow">https://Fundition.io</a> They also do charity projects on the STEEM platform. One can support them directly there by donating STEEM. The difference is, that there is no own token system behind it, that accelerates the circulation of donating and spending. Their focus is on funding projects, our focus is on spending attention and hope also to small charity occasions. One can also combine fundition and NOBEL just by using the hashtag #nobel in the fundition posts.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-six-winning-participants-with-nobel" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#six-winning-participants-with-nobel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Six Winning Participants With NOBEL:</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-1-needy-people" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1-needy-people"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>1. Needy People</h2>
<p>They get help without delivering something. But they should try to get out of the needy situation.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-2-charity-helpers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2-charity-helpers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>2. Charity Helpers</h2>
<p>Now they get rewarded for the job they do. They can (and should) sell (or stake) the NOBEL coins. The only thing they have to do additional is to write and post about their work to create Proof of Charity and therefore trust into the coin. This is important to increase the value. Please use the hashtags #nobel and #steem. People, that do charity, should note how much time and how much money they have spend. That gives us a guess how many NOBEL this person should get. Example (originally taken from <a href="https://steempeak.com/@yohan2on" rel="nofollow">@yohanon</a>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Yohan has bought 12 pairs of shoes for needy children and payed 35 US-Dollars for it. This is worth (with 1 NOBEL=1 STEEM = 0,35 US Dollar/STEEM) = 100 NOBEL for the shoes + further 100 (or whatever he guesses) NOBEL for the effort. He shall write it in his blog (#nobel), what the costs are and then he shall sell 200 NOBEL from his account. After that the supporter can buy 200 Nobel with his FIAT Money to keep the prize stable.
<a href="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/shoes_for_needy_kids.png" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/97b8860158c5aa90f8ecb09bdce6ff4d6a7e0fcd/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30372f73686f65735f666f725f6e656564795f6b6964732e706e67" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/shoes_for_needy_kids.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-3-the-donators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3-the-donators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>3. The Donators</h2>
<p>Donators have with nobel.charity a tool to gift in three ways: <br></p>
<ol>
<li>Directly with maximal efficience: <br>
This means, there is no man in the middle. There are only banking exchange fees (that every NGO has to handle with also). When a donator knows who to support, he can give the NOBEL or STEEM token directly to the recipient. <br></li>
<li>Supporting The Community: <br>
By buying NOBEL and sending it to the distribution bot @anobel, a donator keeps the price high. He puts money into the system. The community distributes NOBEL by upvoting, so the "best" charity helpers get the most token, which they can exchange now for a good value on the market. <br></li>
<li>Gaining influence power:<br>
By buying NOBEL and staking it, the donator gets an investor and curator<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/31b51e71d07342ad50a2efbb6161cd2c57c50ceb/68747470733a2f2f737465656d6974696d616765732e636f6d2f36343078302f68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f534e66584f547a732d33776179735f746f5f646f6e6174655f776974685f6e6f62656c2e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/31b51e71d07342ad50a2efbb6161cd2c57c50ceb/68747470733a2f2f737465656d6974696d616765732e636f6d2f36343078302f68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f534e66584f547a732d33776179735f746f5f646f6e6174655f776974685f6e6f62656c2e6a7067" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://steemitimages.com/640x0/https://files.steempeak.com/file/steempeak/achimmertens/SNfXOTzs-3ways_to_donate_with_nobel.jpg" style="max-width:100%;"></a><br>
<em>Flyer made with canvas by Achim Mertens</em></li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/613c6843ce733c33cea0ddea37afecebf35f1f67/68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f757734354d416c312d696d6167652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/613c6843ce733c33cea0ddea37afecebf35f1f67/68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f757734354d416c312d696d6167652e706e67" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://files.steempeak.com/file/steempeak/achimmertens/uw45MAl1-image.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<em>Moneyflow during donation with NOBEL</em></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-4-the-investors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4-the-investors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>4. The Investors</h2>
<p>The investors can buy new NOBEL and therefore give "real" money to the charity helpers. They can stake the coin and hope in a price raise. With staked NOBEL they can also curate.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-5-the-curators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5-the-curators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>5. The Curators</h2>
<p>Curators are people that have staked NOBEL. They either got it by writing blogs with hashtag #nobel and getting upvotes from other NOBEL-staker or they have been gifted some NOBEL or they have bought it. The more NOBEL they have staked, the more NOBEL are send from the distribution bot to the author and curators (the staked NOBEL are untouched). 5% of the distributed NOBEL go to the curators, 95% to the authors.
They can upvote blogs with the hashtag #nobel to support the helpers without losing own coins. They can upvote blogs to influence the direction for future steps with the NOBEL system. They own a part of the NOBEL system.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-6-the-system-itself-and-the-market-members" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6-the-system-itself-and-the-market-members"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>6. The System Itself And The Market Members</h2>
<p>New members have an ability to invest their money into a system that helps people. So they can win value, if the price rises. And they know, that the money is good invested (even if the price falls). Everyone can write blogs about NOBEL (with #nobel) and when the quality is good they can get upvotes and therefore earn these tokens also. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/30f876b2a7b5d0ee7718dfed5011aad00d5c16a6/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30372f6e6f62656c5f636972636c65732e6a706567"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/30f876b2a7b5d0ee7718dfed5011aad00d5c16a6/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30372f6e6f62656c5f636972636c65732e6a706567" alt="NOBEL_Circles" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/nobel_circles.jpeg" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-some-rules-to-handle-the-nobel-token" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#some-rules-to-handle-the-nobel-token"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Some Rules To Handle The NOBEL Token:</h1>
<ul>
<li><strong>Humanity is more important than greed!!!</strong> It is more important to support charity helpers and needy people than to get rich with the token. Please live this to get trust to the coin.</li>
<li>Give the token (or stake it and upvote ) to people, that have done good things to other people.</li>
<li>When you have done good things,
<ul>
<li>please write about it and use the #nobel tag. It is important that others get aware of it to find supporters, that buy the token.</li>
<li>sell some of your tokens for a good price. This is necessary to create an economic circle and give the token a value.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>When you misuse the #nobel tag for posts, that have nothing to do with charity or promoting NOBEL, you will get a nice comment, a warning or a downvote (that also effects your STEEM reputation).</li>
</ul>
<p>You may think "I want to do good things without knowing others about it". Of course this is also ok, but then you cannot find supporters. Your work would get much more effect, when you have a strong team behind you. Therefore it is necessary to get awareness and to give a good proof that you do a good work by writing blogs about it on the STEEM-platform.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-the-whales-big-investors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-whales-big-investors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>The Whales (Big Investors)</h1>
<p>A smal group of people has got 100,000.00 token in the beginning. They have some additional duties in their own interest:</p>
<ul>
<li>They shall not sell the initial coins for the next 5 years. Therefore all of them have staked their coins.</li>
<li>They should do some advertising and influencing to get value and money into the system.</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-they-get-value-into-nobel" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-they-get-value-into-nobel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>How do they get value into NOBEL?</h2>
<p>It's all about: Find more buyers than sellers. The coin itself has no value at all. The price will drop drastically, when we sell without having buyers. We need to establich a working system, that has value and then the money will follow.
<a href="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/nobel-value.png" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/962fdf1313a8b0425c7c65992f04957ddda41326/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30372f6e6f62656c2d76616c75652e706e67" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/07/nobel-value.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Â  Â  Â 
<em>(left: initial status of NOBEL, right: healthy status of another coin)</em></p>
<p>Achim (the creator of this token) is going to buy,</p>
<ul>
<li>When people do charity (see example above)</li>
<li>max. 80 US Dollar/Month (status 2019/07)</li>
</ul>
<p>If we find more people, that follow the example of Achim, then the budget is higher. We need to sell our "idea", not the token. Each tokenbuyer has to be handled like a customer.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-should-they-upvote" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-should-they-upvote"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>What should they upvote?</h2>
<p>With the upvotes from the whales they further incentivise people that are bringing value into our NOBEL system. This can be advertising/influencing or writing about projects, where the NOBEL coin is involved.
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/74e30d59820fe702e9154796b6c34912dc4b5e9d/68747470733a2f2f737465656d6974696d616765732e636f6d2f3078302f68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f56586e386f7647642d696d6167652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/74e30d59820fe702e9154796b6c34912dc4b5e9d/68747470733a2f2f737465656d6974696d616765732e636f6d2f3078302f68747470733a2f2f66696c65732e737465656d7065616b2e636f6d2f66696c652f737465656d7065616b2f616368696d6d657274656e732f56586e386f7647642d696d6167652e706e67" alt="image.png" data-canonical-src="https://steemitimages.com/0x0/https://files.steempeak.com/file/steempeak/achimmertens/VXn8ovGd-image.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<em>(Sketch by Achim Mertens)</em>
For details about the configuration of the scotbot see <a href="https://steempeak.com/nobel/@achimmertens/the-scotbot-distributes-the-nobel-token-now" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-nobel_faq" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#nobel_faq"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>NOBEL_FAQ:</h1>
<p><strong>Why should I buy NOBEL?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Every time you buy NOBEL, money flows into the system. This money is mentioned for people that do good things. So by buying NOBEL you contribute to "save the world" ;-).</li>
<li>Eliminate the middlemen and some of the transaction fee.</li>
<li>Take over control. Or let a community decide who to support.</li>
<li>Get "Proof of Charity"</li>
</ul>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/201c952be663cfe993929d3c6307219ef6f257ab/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30382f646f6e6174655f6d6f73745f656666696369656e746c792e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/201c952be663cfe993929d3c6307219ef6f257ab/68747470733a2f2f677265656e736e697065722e66696c65732e776f726470726573732e636f6d2f323031392f30382f646f6e6174655f6d6f73745f656666696369656e746c792e6a7067" alt="Donate_most_efficiently" data-canonical-src="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/08/donate_most_efficiently.jpg" style="max-width:100%;"></a> (<a href="https://greensniper.wordpress.com/how-to-donate-most-efficiently/" rel="nofollow">Flyer</a> by Achim Mertens)</p>
<p><strong>What can I do with the NOBEL (use cases)?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>You can gift it to people, that do charity. (See also: "To whom can I gift the NOBEL?")</li>
<li>You can send it to @anobel, the Scotbotaccount. This money is used to be distributed, depending on the upvotes. With this you trust the community to decide, who shall get the most.</li>
<li>You can stake it, to spend it later, when it has (hopefully) more value.</li>
<li>You can sell it (for hopefully a better price).</li>
<li>You can gift NOBEL as a (birthday) present</li>
<li>You can use NOBEL instead of gaming coins (and gift the pot)</li>
<li>You can pay helpers (when they accept it)</li>
<li>... (more ideas welcome)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Who shall buy the NOBEL?</strong>
Everyone can do that. The target group is people, that want to do good things, but don't know how. With buying NOBEL you support charity workers.</p>
<p><strong>How do I get NOBEL?</strong>
You need to have an account on the STEEM blockchain. i.e. you can register here: <a href="https://steemit.com" rel="nofollow">https://steemit.com</a>. Then you need some STEEM. This you can earn by posting and upvoting or you can exchange it on a bank like <a href="https://www.bitpanda.com" rel="nofollow">Bitpanda</a> or <a href="https://coinmerce.io/" rel="nofollow">coinmerce</a>. With this STEEM you can buy tokens likeÂ NOBEL here: <a href="https://steem-engine.com/?p=market&amp;t=NOBEL" rel="nofollow">https://steem-engine.com/?p=market&amp;t=NOBEL</a> You can also join our contests or airdrops to earn NOBEL (and STEEM at the same time).
<a href="https://greensniper.files.wordpress.com/2019/08/howtobuynobeltoken.jpg" rel="nofollow"></a></p>
<p><strong>How does the NOBEL increase in value?</strong>
Sometimes, when you put things together something magic happens: Emergence. For example wind + sand -&gt; wind + sand + dunes. The dunes are the emergence of this system. So it is with tokens that are used by people. The NOBEL was mainly built to create a cash flow from financial supporters to charity supporters . This means, I prognose the following phases (with the precondition, that our marketing works):</p>
<ol>
<li>The price has to find its value (Launch phase July-October 2019)</li>
<li>The price will rise</li>
<li>The price will stabilize</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>How big is the risk when I buy NOBEL?</strong>
In that moment you buy, the price increases, which is good for the charity workers. When you gift the coin, then there is a (normal) risk for you, that the recipient do something other with your money. But with the Proof of Charity concept this risk is minimalized. When you keep it, then there is the normal market risk with every coin. The charity helpers sell the coins as soon as they need money. This keeps the risk of market effects for them low. There is a risk, that people get NOBLE coins by misusing the #noble tag, getting upvoted by others and then selling the coin. This is not the best idea for these people, because they can also get downvotes, which decreases the value of their posts and their (STEEM-) reputation. Especially, when a whale downvotes. But nevertheless, there is a small risk, that people get this coin without deserving it. Let's see in the future how big this effect is. One can observe the NOBEL market here: <a href="https://steem-engine.rocks/transactions?symbol=NOBEL" rel="nofollow">https://steem-engine.rocks/transactions?symbol=NOBEL</a></p>
<p><strong>Do daytraders steel FIAT money?</strong>
It looks like, when you buy NOBEL. You can often see, that you pay for people or bots, that have bought cheap NOBEL and sell them now, when you buy them. This looks like if you support parasits. But on the other hand, they also buy NOBEL and give therefore money to the target group, the charity helpers. To sum it up, they neither win nor loose money here. But they help us to close the gap between ask and bid.</p>
<p><strong>Who is doing the marketing?</strong>
Everyone who is convinced of the NOBEL or thinks it should be given a try. There are some whales that are eager to see the price rising.</p>
<p><strong>How shall we do marketing?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Write about the NOBEL. Post it on every social media (facebook, instagram, twitter, reddit, ...)</li>
<li>Offer contests. I.e.:
<ul>
<li>Â "Show me your Charity work and you will get xxx NOBEL"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We can use the #seven77 movement to make 7 pushups for STEEM and NOBEL</li>
<li>Offer xxx NOBEL each for the first 10 posts about NOBEL</li>
<li>Offer Airdrops. I.e.:
<ul>
<li>Buy 100 Nobel and you get 100 NOBEL extra</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Who shell sell the NOBEL?</strong>
The NOBEL is a free coin on the market, so everyone can sell it. But the aim of this token is, that mainly the people sell it, that have done charity. You can sell (or change) NOBEL here: <a href="https://steem-engine.com/?p=market&amp;t=NOBEL" rel="nofollow">https://steem-engine.com/?p=market&amp;t=NOBEL</a></p>
<p><strong>What makes the NOBEL unique?</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>The NOBEL is an high effective charity distribution tool, where the donators either directly support their favorite charity workers or leave it up to the community to care about, that the money goes to the right places. The charity workers do âProof of Charityâ by writing blogs about their work. STEEM (the base of NOBEL) is a great blockchain platform with a big and good minded community, that creates value by connecting the right people. No NGO or middleman is needed.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>The aim of the token is not mainly to get rich of it or to create financial value (when the price rises and you have staked NOBEL, you can also profit from it monetary), it is more a cashflow: With buying NOBEL, money comes in, with spending money by the charity helpers, money goes out.</p>
<p><strong>To whom can I gift the NOBEL?</strong>
The target group is people that help other people. This can be your neighbor who helps you (or others) in the garden, but also charity helpers somewhere in the world. You can find them with the hashtag #nobel on the <a href="https://steempeak.com/created/nobel" rel="nofollow">steem plattform</a>. But you can also send it to charity groups like <a href="https://steempeak.com/@fundition" rel="nofollow">@fundition</a>,Â <a href="https://steempeak.com/@teamuganda" rel="nofollow">@teamuganda,Â </a>....Â They will use the money like an NGO to support the supporters. Honor people that do good things like in the next question:</p>
<p><strong>What kind of charity can I do to get NOBEL?</strong>
Everything is allowed that helps other people and do not harm someone else. The more work and effort you invest and the more it helps, the more token you should get. So supporting children to get good education is more value than playing football with them. Here are some examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Helping needy children</li>
<li>Giving food or clothes to poor people</li>
<li>paying school fees</li>
<li>Going to demonstrations for liberty or humanity (i.e. #firdaysforfuture)</li>
<li>Help in the neighborhood</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Who are the charity helpers?</strong>
In the beginning it is <a href="https://steempeak.com/@yohan2on" rel="nofollow">@Yohan2on</a>Â (I met him personally in Uganda) <a href="https://steempeak.com/@manchochris" rel="nofollow">@manchochris</a>Â and <a href="https://steemit.com/@muzito08" rel="nofollow">@muzito08</a>.Â  But I hope a lot of people will follow. It can be everyone.</p>
<p><strong>How can I get a charity helper?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Get an account on <a href="https://steemit.com" rel="nofollow">https://steemit.com</a></li>
<li>Do something good to other (needy) people</li>
<li>Write a blog about it on <a href="https://steemit.com" rel="nofollow">https://steemit.com</a> (or another frontend for STEEM)</li>
<li>Show in detail what you did with pictures to create a "Proof of Charity".</li>
<li>Include how much effort and costs you have had for your charity work.</li>
<li>Use the hashtag #nobel (see the example above under "Charity Helpers").
Then you should hopefully get some of the coins.</li>
</ul>

<h1><a id="user-content-general-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#general-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>General</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-steemitcom" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-steemitcom"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_steemit_com">What is steemit.com?</span></h2>
<p>Steemit has redefined social media by building a living, breathing, and growing social economy - a community where users are rewarded for sharing their voice. It's a new kind of attention economy.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-does-steemit-work" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-does-steemit-work"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_does_steemit_work">How does Steemit work?</span></h2>
<p>Steemit.com is one of the many websites (including <a href="https://busy.org/" rel="nofollow">Busy.org</a>, <a href="https://d.tube/" rel="nofollow">DTube</a>, and <a href="https://steempeak.com/" rel="nofollow">SteemPeak.com</a>) that are powered by the Steem blockchain and STEEM cryptocurrency. All of these websites read and write content to the Steem blockchain, which stores the content in an immutable blockchain ledger, and rewards users for their contributions with digital tokens called STEEM.</p>
<p>Every day, the Steem blockchain mints new STEEM tokens and adds them to a community's "rewards pool". These tokens are then awarded to users for their contributions, based on the votes that their content receives. Users who hold more tokens in their account as "Steem Power" will get to decide where a larger portion of the rewards pool is distributed.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-does-steemit-differ-from-other-social-media-websites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-does-steemit-differ-from-other-social-media-websites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_does_steemit_differ_from_other_social_media_websites">How does Steemit differ from other social media websites?</span></h2>
<p>While most social media sites extract this value for the benefit of their shareholders, Steemit believes that the users of the platform should receive the benefits and rewards for their attention and the contributions they make to the platform.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-do-i-need-to-do-in-order-to-secure-my-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-do-i-need-to-do-in-order-to-secure-my-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_do_i_need_to_do_in_order_to_secure_my_account">What do I need to do in order to secure my account?</span></h2>
<p>Unlike most social media websites, <strong>there is no way to recover your account if you lose your password / owner key!</strong> This is why it is extremely important that you save and backup your password somewhere safe. It is strongly recommended that you store an offline copy in case of a hard drive failure or other calamity. Consider digital offline storage, such as an external disk or flash drive, as well as printed paper stored in a fireproof safe. Use a safe deposit box for best redundancy.</p>
<p>If you leak your private key to another user or a third-party website, that user or website will have full access to your account. This means they can steal it, as well as the funds inside of it. It is therefore not recommended to enter your private key information with any other user or third-party website. If you believe your account has been compromised, you should change your password/keys right away.</p>
<p>Each account has multiple keys, which each have different levels of authority: owner, active, posting, and memo. The information on the different types of keys and their purposes, as well as more information on password and key security, can be found in the section on <a href="#Table_of_Contents_Security">Security</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-does-it-cost-anything-to-post-comment-or-vote" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#does-it-cost-anything-to-post-comment-or-vote"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-does_it_cost_anything_to_post__comment__or_vote">Does it cost anything to post, comment, or vote?</span></h2>
<p>No. It is free to post, comment, and vote on content on steemit.com. You might even get paid for it!</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-earn-digital-tokens-on-steemit-how" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-earn-digital-tokens-on-steemit-how"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_earn_digital_tokens_on_steemit_how">Can I earn digital tokens on Steemit? How?</span></h2>
<p>You can earn digital tokens on Steemit by:</p>
<p><strong>Posting</strong> - By sharing your posts, you can earn upvotes from community members. Depending on the upvotes you receive, you may get a portion of the "rewards pool".</p>
<p><strong>Voting and curating</strong> - If you discover a post and upvote it before it becomes popular, you can earn a curation reward. The reward amount will depend on the amount of Steem Power you have.</p>
<p><strong>Purchasing</strong> - Users can purchase STEEM or Steem Dollar tokens directly through their Steemit wallet using bitcoin, Ether, or BitShares tokens. They are also available from other markets and exchanges including <a href="https://www.binance.com/" rel="nofollow">Binance</a>, <a href="https://www.bithumb.com/" rel="nofollow">Bithumb</a>, <a href="https://wallet.bitshares.org/" rel="nofollow">BitShares</a>, <a href="https://bittrex.com" rel="nofollow">Bittrex</a>, <a href="https://blocktrades.us" rel="nofollow">BlockTrades</a>, <a href="https://changelly.com" rel="nofollow">Changelly</a>, <a href="https://www.gobaba.com/" rel="nofollow">GOBADA</a>, <a href="https://www.gopax.co.kr" rel="nofollow">GOPAX</a>, <a href="https://hitbtc.com/" rel="nofollow">HitBTC</a>, <a href="https://www.huobi.pro/" rel="nofollow">Huobi</a>, <a href="https://www.localbitcoincash.org/" rel="nofollow">LocalBitcoinCash</a>, <a href="https://poloniex.com" rel="nofollow">Poloniex</a>, <a href="https://shapeshift.io" rel="nofollow">Shapeshift.io</a>, <a href="https://upbit.com/" rel="nofollow">UpBit</a>, and <a href="https://yensesa.com" rel="nofollow">Yensesa</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Vesting</strong> - STEEM tokens that are powered up to Steem Power will earn a small amount of new tokens for holding.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-where-do-the-tokens-come-from" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#where-do-the-tokens-come-from"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-where_do_the_tokens_come_from">Where do the tokens come from?</span></h2>
<p>The Steem network continually creates new digital tokens to reward content creators and curators. Some of the newly-created tokens are transferred to users who add value to Steem by posting, commenting, and voting on other people's posts. The remainder is distributed to holders of Steem Power and the witnesses that power the blockchain.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-where-does-the-value-come-from" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#where-does-the-value-come-from"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-where_does_the_value_come_from">Where does the value come from?</span></h2>
<p>At its root, Steem is simply a points system. However, because this points system is blockchain-based, the points can be traded on markets as tokens. People buy and sell these tokens, and many hold in anticipation of increased purchasing power for various Steem-related services.</p>
<p>By analogy, Steem is a game system where users compete for attention and rewards by bringing content and adding value to the platform. The rewards people earn are tokens that have market value and are readily tradable. It is similar to how someone playing a video game could obtain a limited item or currency by playing the game. If the currency or items are transferable between users, then they can sell or buy them on game item markets.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-why-are-people-getting-vastly-different-rewards" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#why-are-people-getting-vastly-different-rewards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-why_are_people_getting_vastly_different_rewards">Why are people getting vastly different rewards?</span></h2>
<p>Steemit is not a "get rich quick" scheme. While it is possible to post content that goes viral quickly and earn a lot of rewards on a single post, this is not typical for most users.</p>
<p>Most of the authors that you see earning high rewards are users that have spent a lot of time in the network building followings, making connections with others, and developing a reputation for bringing high quality content.</p>
<p>It is best to have realistic expectations, without focusing on rewards when you are first starting out. Work on building a following, making connections, and developing a good reputation. Consistency will pay off in the long run.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-is-there-a-desktop-wallet-available-for-steem" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#is-there-a-desktop-wallet-available-for-steem"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-is_there_a_desktop_wallet_available_for_steem">Is there a desktop wallet available for STEEM?</span></h2>
<p>Yes. There is a third party wallet called <a href="https://github.com/aaroncox/vessel/">Vessel</a>, developed by one of the Steem witnesses @jesta. The latest release can be downloaded <a href="https://github.com/aaroncox/vessel/releases">here</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-are-smart-media-tokens-smts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-are-smart-media-tokens-smts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_are_smart_media_tokens_smts">What are Smart Media Tokens (SMTs)?</span></h2>
<p>A Smart Media Token (SMT) is a native digital asset on the Steem blockchain that can be quickly launched by anyone to help monetize online content and create incentives to encourage desired user behavior.</p>
<p>They're like Ethereum's ERC-20 tokens, but with certain built-in âProof-of-Brainâ properties and a token distribution reward system designed specifically for digital content businesses.</p>
<p>SMTs are planned to be launched in 2020!</p>
<p>More information can be found on the SMTs website: <a href="https://smt.steem.io/" rel="nofollow">smt.steem.io</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_General">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-accounts-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#accounts-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Accounts</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-create-an-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-create-an-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_create_an_account">How do I create an account?</span></h2>
<p>Click on the "Sign Up" link at the top of steemit.com to get started.</p>
<p>You will be asked to enter your email address and verify your phone number. After your information has been verified, you will be added to the waiting list to receive an account. You will be notified via email once your account is approved.</p>
<p>After you receive notification that your account is approved, click on the link in the email to finish the account creation process. <strong>Be sure to save and backup your username and password.</strong> It is very important that you do not lose your password. There is no way to recover your password or access your account if it is lost. Once your password is saved and backed up, click on the "Create Account" button to create the account.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-information-do-i-need-to-provide-in-order-to-create-an-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-information-do-i-need-to-provide-in-order-to-create-an-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_information_do_i_need_to_provide_in_order_to_create_an_account">What information do I need to provide in order to create an account?</span></h2>
<p>You will need to provide your email address and phone number.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-long-does-the-account-approval-process-take" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-long-does-the-account-approval-process-take"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_long_does_the_account_approval_process_take">How long does the account approval process take?</span></h2>
<p>Some accounts are approved faster than others. Most accounts are approved within 24 hours. Some may take a week or two to review.</p>
<p>If your account has not been approved after more than two weeks, you can ask for help in the <a href="https://steem.chat/channel/help" rel="nofollow">#help</a> channel on <a href="https://steem.chat/home" rel="nofollow">steem.chat</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-speed-up-the-account-approval-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-speed-up-the-account-approval-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_speed_up_the_account_approval_process">Can I speed up the account approval process?</span></h2>
<p>There is currently no way to speed up the account approval process. If you are unable to wait, there are third-party websites listed below that allow you to bypass the approval process and pay to open an account.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-why-do-i-need-to-provide-my-email-and-phone-number" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#why-do-i-need-to-provide-my-email-and-phone-number"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-why_do_i_need_to_provide_my_email_and_phone_number">Why do I need to provide my email and phone number?</span></h2>
<p>To create an account on the blockchain, it costs STEEM tokens. When you create an account through steemit.com, Steemit Inc. is supplying the tokens to pay the account creation fee. In order to prevent users from abusing the paid-for signup and creating multiple accounts, we need to be able to verify that each user is only signing up for one account.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-create-a-steem-account-without-an-email-and-phone-number" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-create-a-steem-account-without-an-email-and-phone-number"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_create_a_steem_account_without_an_email_and_phone_number">Can I create a Steem account without an email and phone number?</span></h2>
<p>The only way to have an account created via steemit.com is to supply your email and phone number. Because Steem is an open and permissionless network, there are other ways to create an account. Any Steem blockchain account can be used on steemit.com.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-are-other-ways-to-create-an-account-on-the-blockchain-besides-using-steemitcom" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-are-other-ways-to-create-an-account-on-the-blockchain-besides-using-steemitcom"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_are_other_ways_to_create_an_account_on_the_blockchain_besides_using_steemit_com">What are other ways to create an account on the blockchain besides using steemit.com?</span></h2>
<p>If you are willing to pay your own signup fee, then there are other ways to create a new account on the blockchain.</p>
<p>There is a third-party tool called <a href="https://www.SteemCreate.com" rel="nofollow">SteemCreate</a> that accepts credit cards, or BTC to create a Steem account. You do not need to have an existing Steem blockchain account to use the service, but there is a charge on top of the blockchain account creation fee for using the service.</p>
<p>There is a third-party tool called <a href="https://blocktrades.us/create-steem-account" rel="nofollow">BlockTrades</a> that accepts bitcoin, Litecoin, STEEM, SBD, BitShares, Dash, Dogecoin, Ethereum, and more to create a Steem account. You can also send extra tokens to pre-load the account with additional Steem Power. You do not need to have an existing Steem blockchain account to use the service, but there is a charge on top of the blockchain account creation fee for using the service.</p>
<p>There is a third-party tool called <a href="https://anon.steem.network/" rel="nofollow">AnonSteem</a> that accepts bitcoin, Litecoin, STEEM, or SBD to anonymously create a Steem account. You do not need to have an existing Steem blockchain account to use the service, but there is a charge on top of the blockchain account creation fee for using the service.</p>
<p>There is a third-party tool called <a href="https://steemit.com/news/@timcliff/new-tool-from-busy-org-create-new-steem-blockchain-accounts-with-steemconnect" rel="nofollow">SteemConnect</a> that allows you to create accounts by paying or delegating the account creation fee. There is no additional fee to use the service, but does require an existing Steem blockchain account to pay the account creation fee to create the account.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-it-is-not-letting-me-create-an-account-with-my-phone-number-what-should-i-do" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#it-is-not-letting-me-create-an-account-with-my-phone-number-what-should-i-do"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-it_is_not_letting_me_create_an_account_with_my_phone_number__what_should_i_do">It is not letting me create an account with my phone number. What should I do?</span></h2>
<p>Ask for help in the <a href="https://steem.chat/channel/help" rel="nofollow">#help</a> channel on <a href="https://steem.chat/home" rel="nofollow">steem.chat</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-happens-if-my-email-or-phone-number-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-happens-if-my-email-or-phone-number-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_happens_if_my_email_or_phone_number_changes">What happens if my email or phone number changes?</span></h2>
<p>Currently there is no way to change the email or phone number that is linked to your account.  Though once your account is created, you can continue to use it even if the email or phone number that is linked to the account has changed.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-am-i-allowed-to-create-more-than-one-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#am-i-allowed-to-create-more-than-one-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-am_i_allowed_to_create_more_than_one_account">Am I allowed to create more than one account?</span></h2>
<p>Each user is allowed only one paid-for account created via steemit.com, however users are allowed to create as many accounts as they want on the blockchain. Creating additional accounts on the blockchain requires users to pay their own account creation fee using one of the third-party services listed above.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-change-my-username" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-change-my-username"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_change_my_username">Can I change my username?</span></h2>
<p>Account names can not be changed. If you would like a new account name, you must pay to create a new account using a third-party account creation service.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-delete-or-deactivate-my-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-delete-or-deactivate-my-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_delete_or_deactivate_my_account">Can I delete or deactivate my account?</span></h2>
<p>Accounts can not be deactivated or deleted. The account along with all of its activity is permanently stored in the blockchain.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Accounts">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-community-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#community-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Community</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-is-there-an-etiquette-guide-for-steemit" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#is-there-an-etiquette-guide-for-steemit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-is_there_an_etiquette_guide_for_steemit">Is there an Etiquette Guide for Steemit?</span></h2>
<p>There are no official rules for participating on steemit.com, but one of the users @thecryptofiend has created an <a href="https://steemit.com/steemit/@thecryptofiend/the-complete-steemit-etiquette-guide-revision-2-0" rel="nofollow">Etiquette Guide</a> for the community. While it is not required to follow the suggestions in the guide, they are standards that many users in the community choose to follow.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Community">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-am-i-required-to-verify-my-identity" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#am-i-required-to-verify-my-identity"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-am_i_required_to_verify_my_identity">Am I required to verify my identity?</span></h2>
<p>Verification is a process where users give evidence to show that they are the person that they claim to be.  This is to reduce fraud and people impersonating known figures. If you would like to remain anonymous, that is perfectly fine. However if you claim to be someone specific, the community may expect that you verify you are who you say you are.</p>
<p>There are a number of ways to do this. The most common way to verify your identity is by posting a link to your Steemit profile on a website or social media account which you are already known for having such as Twitter, Facebook, LinkedIn, a blog, or photography site.</p>
<p>Many users also like to post a photo or a video which shows them holding up a sheet of paper with the current date and their Steem account name handwritten on it. This is a great way to add a personal touch to verifying.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Community">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-site-navigation-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#site-navigation-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Site Navigation</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-upvote-a-post-or-comment" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-upvote-a-post-or-comment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_upvote_a_post_or_comment">How do I upvote a post or comment?</span></h2>
<p>To upvote a post or comment, click on the "upvote" icon at the bottom of the post/comment. </p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
