<h2><a id="user-content-what-do-the-home-new-hot-trending-and-promoted-links-show" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-do-the-home-new-hot-trending-and-promoted-links-show"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_do_the_home__new__hot__trending__and_promoted_links_show">What do the Home, New, Hot, Trending, and Promoted links show?</span></h2>
<p>These are various ways to sort Steem posts.</p>
<p><strong>Home</strong> - The most recent posts of the accounts you follow (your feed).</p>
<p><strong>New</strong> - Posts are sorted by the time posted, with newest first.</p>
<p><strong>Hot</strong> - Popular posts at the moment.</p>
<p><strong>Trending</strong> - Posts with the most amount of votes, stake-weighted, recently.</p>
<p><strong>Promoted</strong> - Listings that are boosted by Steem Dollar payments get promoted for greater visibility.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-information-is-available-in-my-account-menu" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-information-is-available-in-my-account-menu"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_information_is_available_in_my_account_menu">What information is available in my account menu?</span></h2>
<p>You can get to your account menu by clicking on the avatar icon in the top-right corner of a steemit.com page.</p>
<p><strong>Feed</strong> - Here is where you go to see the most recent posts from the people you follow.</p>
<p><strong>Blog</strong> - Here is where you go to see all of your posts and resteems. It is also where you go to see your profile page that is viewable by other users.</p>
<p><strong>Comments</strong> - Here is where you go to see all of the comments and replies you have made.</p>
<p><strong>Replies</strong> - Here is where you go to see all replies other users have made to your posts and comments.</p>
<p><strong>Toggle Night Mode</strong> - This will toggle the steemit.com website views between "night" and "day" mode themes.</p>
<p><strong>Wallet</strong> - This will take you to <a href="https://steemitwallet.com" rel="nofollow">steemitwallet.com</a>, where you go to see your wallet balances, make transfers, exchange STEEM or Steem Dollars, manage your account, and Power Up.</p>
<p><strong>Settings</strong> - Here is where you go to update your settings.</p>
<p><strong>Logout</strong> - If you'd like to logout.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-see-my-recent-rewards" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-see-my-recent-rewards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_see_my_recent_rewards">How do I see my recent rewards?</span></h2>
<p>The Rewards drop-down menu is available on <a href="https://steemitwallet.com" rel="nofollow">steemitwallet.com</a>. Click it and there are two links:</p>
<p><strong>Curation rewards</strong> - Shows the rewards earned for upvoting posts and comments.</p>
<p><strong>Author rewards</strong> - Shows the rewards earned by your own posts and comments.</p>
<p>You can also view the same information for other users by visiting their wallet profile.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-information-is-shown-in-my-wallet" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-information-is-shown-in-my-wallet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_information_is_shown_in_my_wallet">What information is shown in my wallet?</span></h2>
<p>Your <a href="https://steemitwallet.com" rel="nofollow">steemitwallet.com</a> wallet shows how many STEEM and Steem Dollar tokens you have in your account. It shows how much Steem Power it has, and how much SP is delegated. It also shows how many of your STEEM and Steem Dollar tokens are being held in the savings account, which is a balance that is subject to 3 day withdraw waiting period. The wallet page shows any the progress of any Steem Dollar to STEEM conversions as well as the status of a power down. It also shows an estimated value of all the tokens in your account, based on the recent market price of STEEM.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-transfer-my-steem-or-steem-dollars-into-savings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-transfer-my-steem-or-steem-dollars-into-savings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_transfer_my_steem_or_steem_dollars_into_savings">How do I transfer my STEEM or Steem Dollars into savings?</span></h2>
<p>Your savings balance is STEEM and SBD tokens that are subject to 3 day withdraw waiting period. This is an extra security measure in case your account credentials are compromised. To transfer STEEM or SBD tokens into savings, click on the drop-down arrow next to STEEM or STEEM DOLLARS in your wallet, and select "Transfer to Savings".</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-send-money-to-another-user" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-send-money-to-another-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_send_money_to_another_user">How do I send money to another user?</span></h2>
<ul>
<li>From your wallet page, click the STEEM or Steem Dollar balances with the down arrow next to them.</li>
<li>In the drop-down menu, click 'Transfer'.</li>
<li>Type the username of the account you want to send the STEEM or Steem Dollars to. Double and triple check the spelling.</li>
<li>Enter the amount of STEEM or Steem Dollars to send.</li>
<li>Enter a memo to go along with the transaction (optional).</li>
<li>Click Submit.</li>
<li>You will be prompted for your password. You will need to enter your master password or active key.</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-will-i-receive-notifications-when-there-is-activity-with-my-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#will-i-receive-notifications-when-there-is-activity-with-my-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-will_i_receive_notifications_when_there_is_activity_with_my_account">Will I receive notifications when there is activity with my account?</span></h2>
<p>Notifications are currently not supported, but they are a feature we are planning to add.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-shown-in-my-profile" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-shown-in-my-profile"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_shown_in_my_profile">What is shown in my profile?</span></h2>
<p>At the top of your profile is your display name and reputation score. Below your display name is the number of followers you have, the number of posts and comments you have written, and the number of people you are following. It also shows the month and year when your account was created.</p>
<p>You have the option to change your avatar and display name on the <a href="https://steemitwallet.com" rel="nofollow">steemitwallet.com</a> Settings page. There, you can set additional information such as "about" information, your location, and add a link to a website of your choosing. You also have the option to set a cover image for your profile.</p>
<p>You can view your own profile by clicking on the link to your Blog in your account menu.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-change-my-avatar-image-and-other-profile-information" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-change-my-avatar-image-and-other-profile-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_change_my_avatar_image_and_other_profile_information">How do I change my avatar image and other profile information?</span></h2>
<p>Your profile info, avatar image, and cover image are set in your <a href="https://steemitwallet.com" rel="nofollow">steemitwallet.com</a> Settings page. In order to update your avatar picture and cover image, you will need to host the images somewhere. This can be done by uploading it via the wallet GUI, or using a third-party image hosting site such as <a href="http://postimage.io/" rel="nofollow">Postimage</a>.  Once your image is uploaded, copy its URL and paste it into the "Profile Picture URL" box for the avatar, or the "Cover Image URL" box for the cover image. Then click the Update button and enter your password or active key.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-the-recommend-size-for-the-cover-image" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-the-recommend-size-for-the-cover-image"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_the_recommend_size_for_the_cover_image">What is the recommend size for the cover image?</span></h2>
<p>The cover image will be resized/scaled depending on the device being used. Therefore it is recommend to use an image that will still look good when cropped or resized. A 2048x512 image is the optimal size to work for most devices.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-can-i-control-whether-i-see-not-safe-for-work-nsfw-content" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-can-i-control-whether-i-see-not-safe-for-work-nsfw-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_can_i_control_whether_i_see__not_safe_for_work___nsfw__content">How can I control whether I see "Not Safe For Work" (NSFW) content?</span></h2>
<p>By default, content that users have tagged as "NSFW" will be hidden, but a link will be shown to reveal the content.</p>
<p>You can update your display preference with the Settings page so that NSFW content is always shown by default, remains hidden until clicked, or is completely hidden with no option to reveal.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-search-for-content" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-search-for-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_search_for_content">How do I search for content?</span></h2>
<p>In the upper right corner of Steemit, there is a magnifying glass search link where you can find posts using a keyword search.</p>
<p>There is also an <strong>Explore</strong> link in the main menu, where you can browse through posts based on tags.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-see-which-users-i-have-muted" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-see-which-users-i-have-muted"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_see_which_users_i_have_muted">Can I see which users I have muted?</span></h2>
<p>Yes. This can be seen under the Settings page.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-see-which-users-have-muted-me" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-see-which-users-have-muted-me"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_see_which_users_have_muted_me">Can I see which users have muted me?</span></h2>
<p>No. This information is not presented on steemit.com.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-see-the-list-of-users-i-am-following-and-who-is-following-me" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-see-the-list-of-users-i-am-following-and-who-is-following-me"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_see_the_list_of_users_i_am_following__and_who_is_following_me">Can I see the list of users I am following, and who is following me?</span></h2>
<p>Yes. You can see the list of followers or people you are following by clicking on the links on your profile page.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-languages-are-supported" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-languages-are-supported"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_languages_are_supported">What languages are supported?</span></h2>
<p>Currently steemit.com supports English, Spanish, Russian, French, Italian, Korean, Polish, and Chinese. There are also many communities using the platform that speak other languages. If you are interested in joining our translation team to add additional languages or help support the ones we have, please email us at <a href="mailto:translate@steemit.com">translate@steemit.com</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Site_Navigation">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-posting-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#posting-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Posting</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-can-users-post-to-steemit" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-can-users-post-to-steemit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_can_users_post_to_steemit">What can users post to Steemit?</span></h2>
<p>Steem is an open platform meant to host and welcome any legal content that complies with our <a href="/hive-engine/nitrous/blob/scotty_nobel/tos.html">terms of service</a>. Users can post anything they want, whether it be phrases, quotes, blogs, anecdotes, photos, videos, memes, songs, and more. Be creative!</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-are-the-different-choices-for-post-rewards-5050-power-up-100-decline-payout" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-are-the-different-choices-for-post-rewards-5050-power-up-100-decline-payout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_are_the_different_choices_for_post_rewards__50__50___power_up_100___decline_payout">What are the different choices for post rewards (50%/50%, Power Up 100%, Decline Payout)?</span></h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>50%/50%</strong> - This rewards in half Steem Power, and half liquid STEEM / Steem Dollars. The ratio of liquid STEEM to Steem Dollars rewarded is based on network conditions at the time of payout. This is the default payout option.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Power Up 100%</strong> - This option rewards the post in 100% Steem Power.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Decline Payout</strong> - Use this option to receive no post rewards. Votes will affect the post's position on the trending ranking but no rewards are paid from Steem's reward pool. Replies made to the post are still eligible for rewards.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-add-images-and-photos-to-my-posts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-add-images-and-photos-to-my-posts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_add_images_and_photos_to_my_posts">How do I add images and photos to my posts?</span></h2>
<p>You can browse your hard drive to add an image by clicking on the "selecting them" link from within the editor.</p>
<p>If you have an image copied to your clipboard, you can simply paste (<code>ctrl + v</code>) while in the post/comment editor, and your image will be uploaded into your post or comment. Due to the file size of these pasted images, this method is only recommended for simple graphics. Photos (.JPG) should be uploaded from your disk.</p>
<p>Pictures can also be hosted on an external site. Paste the image's web address (URL) into the editor and it will automatically be added.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-set-the-thumbnail-image-for-my-post" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-set-the-thumbnail-image-for-my-post"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_set_the_thumbnail_image_for_my_post">How do I set the thumbnail image for my post?</span></h2>
<p>The first image in the post will automatically be set as the thumbnail image.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-the-recommend-aspect-ratio-for-thumbnail-images" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-the-recommend-aspect-ratio-for-thumbnail-images"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_the_recommend_aspect_ratio_for_thumbnail_images">What is the recommend aspect ratio for thumbnail images?</span></h2>
<p>The recommend aspect ratio for thumbnail images is 16x9.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-add-videos-to-my-posts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-add-videos-to-my-posts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_add_videos_to_my_posts">How do I add videos to my posts?</span></h2>
<p>To add a DTube, YouTube, or Vimeo video to your blog post, simply paste the URL link to the video into the post.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-is-there-a-way-i-can-make-my-images-smaller" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#is-there-a-way-i-can-make-my-images-smaller"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-is_there_a_way_i_can_make_my_images_smaller">Is there a way I can make my images smaller?</span></h2>
<p>Yes, but the picture must be resized before it is uploaded into the steemit.com editor. This can be done in your favorite photo editing software, or online by uploading to a third-party website that features editing such as imgur.com.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-are-tags" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-are-tags"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_are_tags">What are tags?</span></h2>
<p>Tags are a way to categorize your content, so that others can find it. The more relevant the tags are to the post, the more like-minded people will come across it.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-tags-should-i-use" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-tags-should-i-use"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_tags_should_i_use">What tags should I use?</span></h2>
<p>Try to use tags that are relevant to your post, and that will be popular for other people to browse. For example, "mytriptoalaska" may be relevant to your post, but readers are probably not going to go searching for that. Using "travel" would be a better choice for a tag in this case.</p>
<p>You can browse through commonly used tags using the "Explore" link, in the main menu.</p>
<p>Be mindful when choosing tags. If your tags arenât related to your post, your post may get downvotes for mistagging.</p>
<p>All tags must be lowercase letters. Spaces aren't allowed, but hyphenated words with a single dash are.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-many-tags-can-i-use" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-many-tags-can-i-use"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_many_tags_can_i_use">How many tags can I use?</span></h2>
<p>You can use up to 8 tags per post.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-why-is-the-post-button-grayed-out" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#why-is-the-post-button-grayed-out"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-why_is_the_post_button_grayed_out">Why is the "Post" button grayed out?</span></h2>
<p>A post must have a title, body, and at least one valid tag. If any of these are missing, then the "Post" button will be disabled.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-format-text-in-markdown" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-format-text-in-markdown"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_format_text_in_markdown">How do I format text in Markdown?</span></h2>
<p>Some common markdown syntax is:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>**bold**</code> <strong>bold</strong></li>
<li><code>_italics_</code> <em>italics</em></li>
<li><code>~~cross out~~</code> <del>cross out</del></li>
</ul>
<p>Text can be sized using headers:</p>
<pre><code># H1
## H2
### H3
#### H4
</code></pre>
<h1><a id="user-content-h1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>H1</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-h2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>H2</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-h3" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>H3</h3>
<h4><a id="user-content-h4" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#h4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>H4</h4>
<p>Instructions on how to justify text, as well as wrap text around images pulled to the left or right can be found in <a href="https://steemit.com/steemit/@steemitblog/new-advanced-formatting-features" rel="nofollow">this guide</a>.</p>
<p>For more advanced formatting, a guide describing the common markdown formatting syntax can be found here: <a href="https://github.com/adam-p/markdown-here/wiki/Markdown-Cheatsheet">Markdown Cheatsheet</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-often-can-i-post" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-often-can-i-post"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_often_can_i_post">How often can I post?</span></h2>
<p>You are allowed to post almost as often as you like. Currently, posts must be spaced 5 minutes apart. However, the community may not find value in users that are posting too frequently. Keep in mind what your audience will be interested in viewing, so that you do not overwhelm your followers with too much content.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-long-can-my-post-be" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-long-can-my-post-be"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_long_can_my_post_be">How long can my post be?</span></h2>
<p>Post sizes are limited to about 64,000 characters including formatting. This is ample for most posts. If writing blogs, consider how much people are willing to read at one time. If you make your posts too long, readers may lose interest which may affect the amount of upvotes and rewards you receive.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-if-posting-in-a-language-other-than-english-how-will-i-get-recognized" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#if-posting-in-a-language-other-than-english-how-will-i-get-recognized"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-if_posting_in_a_language_other_than_english__how_will_i_get_recognized">If posting in a language other than English, how will I get recognized?</span></h2>
<p>You can use language-specific tags to help you to reach the audience that speaks your language.</p>
<p>Language-specific groups include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Chinese = cn</li>
<li>German = deutsch</li>
<li>Spanish = spanish</li>
<li>Korean = kr</li>
<li>Russian = ru</li>
<li>French = fr</li>
<li>Portuguese = pt</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-delete-something-i-posted" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-delete-something-i-posted"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_delete_something_i_posted">Can I delete something I posted?</span></h2>
<p>The blockchain will always contain the full edit history of posts and comments, so it can never be completely deleted. If you would like to update a post so that users cannot see the content via steemit.com, you can edit the post and replace it with blank content for as long as the post is active. After seven days, the post can no longer be edited via steemit.com.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-does-promoting-a-post-do" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-does-promoting-a-post-do"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_does__promoting__a_post_do">What does "Promoting" a post do?</span></h2>
<p>When you make a post, there is the option to promote it with Steem Dollars. It will then show up in the âPromotedâ tab. The order that it appears in the list depends on how much the post was promoted for. Posts with a higher promoted amount will be higher than posts with less.</p>
<p>Steem Dollars spent to promote a post are paid to the account @null, which nobody owns or controls. Once a user transfers SBD to @null, the Steem blockchain removes them from the currency supply. Details can be found in this <a href="https://steemit.com/steemit/@steemitblog/introducing-promoted-content" rel="nofollow">official post</a>.</p>
<p>You can promote your own posts, or posts that you like from other users.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-promote-a-post" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-promote-a-post"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_promote_a_post">How do I promote a post?</span></h2>
<p>At the bottom of each post is a button to "Promote". After clicking the button, type the number of Steem Dollars that you want to spend and click âPROMOTEâ. The operation will require your master password or active key.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Posting">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-comments-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#comments-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Comments</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-earn-digital-tokens-for-commenting" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-earn-digital-tokens-for-commenting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_earn_digital_tokens_for_commenting">Can I earn digital tokens for commenting?</span></h2>
<p>Yes, comments that are upvoted can earn rewards just like posts!</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Comments">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-often-can-i-comment" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-often-can-i-comment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_often_can_i_comment">How often can I comment?</span></h2>
<p>There is a three second wait time in between comments to limit spam.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Comments">^</a></p>
<h1><a id="user-content-economics-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#economics-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Economics</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-where-do-the-new-steem-tokens-come-from" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#where-do-the-new-steem-tokens-come-from"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-where_do_the_new_steem_tokens_come_from">Where do the new STEEM tokens come from?</span></h2>
<p>Blockchains like Steem and Bitcoin produce new tokens each time a block is produced. Unlike Bitcoin, where all of the new coins go to the block producers (called miners), the Steem blockchain allocates a majority of the new tokens to a reward fund called the "rewards pool". The rewards pool gives users tokens for participating in the platform based on the value they add.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-many-new-tokens-are-generated-by-the-blockchain" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-many-new-tokens-are-generated-by-the-blockchain"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_many_new_tokens_are_generated_by_the_blockchain">How many new tokens are generated by the blockchain?</span></h2>
<p>Starting with the network's 16th hard fork in December 2016, Steem began creating new tokens at a yearly inflation rate of 9.5%. The inflation rate decreases at a rate of 0.01% every 250,000 blocks, or about 0.5% per year. The inflation will continue decreasing at this pace until the overall inflation rate reaches 0.95%. This will take about 20.5 years from the time hard fork 16 went into effect.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-are-the-new-tokens-distributed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-are-the-new-tokens-distributed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_are_the_new_tokens_distributed">How are the new tokens distributed?</span></h2>
<p>Out of the new tokens that are generated:</p>
<ul>
<li>65% go to the reward pool, which is split between authors and curators.</li>
<li>15% of the new tokens are awarded to holders of Steem Power.</li>
<li>10% of the new tokens are awarded to the Steem Proposal System.</li>
<li>The remaining 10% pays for the witnesses to power the blockchain.</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-which-exchanges-are-steem-and-sbd-listed-on" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#which-exchanges-are-steem-and-sbd-listed-on"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-which_exchanges_are_steem_and_sbd_listed_on">Which exchanges are STEEM and SBD listed on?</span></h2>

<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-the-reward-pool" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-the-reward-pool"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_the_reward_pool">What is the reward pool?</span></h2>
<p>Every day, a fixed amount of STEEM tokens are allocated to the network reward fund, commonly called the "reward pool." These get distributed to authors and curators for posting and voting on content.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-is-the-reward-pool-split-between-authors-and-curators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-is-the-reward-pool-split-between-authors-and-curators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_is_the_reward_pool_split_between_authors_and_curators">How is the reward pool split between authors and curators?</span></h2>
<p>Up to 50% of a post's payout is awarded to curators (the people who upvoted the post) as a reward for discovering the content. The other 50% is awarded to the author.</p>
<p>If curators vote for a post within the first 5 minutes of it being created, a portion of their curation reward remains in the rewards pool for other authors/curators. This portion is linear to the age of the post between 0 and 5 minutes. As an example: upvoting at two minutes will donate 60% of your potential curation reward back to the rewards pool.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-will-the-reward-pool-pay-out-more-or-less-depending-on-who-votes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#will-the-reward-pool-pay-out-more-or-less-depending-on-who-votes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-will_the_reward_pool_pay_out_more_or_less_depending_on_who_votes">Will the reward pool pay out more or less depending on who votes?</span></h2>
<p>There is a fixed amount of STEEM coins that gets added to the rewards pool each day. In the short term, the amount of coins that get paid out may be higher or lower depending on the amount of voting activity, but over time it will pay out the full amount of rewards regardless of who votes.</p>
<p>Votes in Steem are stake-weighted. Therefore voters with more Steem Power have a greater influence over the allocation than voters with less SP, but their votes do not increase the amount of rewards in the rewards pool.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-why-do-the-earnings-for-my-post-go-up-or-down" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#why-do-the-earnings-for-my-post-go-up-or-down"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-why_do_the_earnings_for_my_post_go_up_or_down">Why do the earnings for my post go up or down?</span></h2>
<p>The amount that is shown next to a post is a "<strong>Potential Payout</strong>". This is an estimated value of how much money the post will make based on the votes that have occurred so far. Depending on various factors, this value can go up or down until the payout window closes:</p>
<ul>
<li>If a post receives more upvotes, the potential payout of the post can go up.</li>
<li>If a post receives more downvotes, the potential payout of the post can go down.</li>
<li>If other posts receive more upvotes, the potential payout of the post can go down.</li>
<li>If other posts receive more downvotes, the potential payout of the post can go up.</li>
<li>If upvotes are removed from a post, the potential payout of the post can go down.</li>
<li>If downvotes are removed from a post, the potential payout of the post can go up.</li>
<li>If the price of STEEM goes up, the potential payout of all posts can go up.</li>
<li>If the price of STEEM goes down, the potential payout of all posts can go down.</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-when-can-i-claim-my-rewards" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#when-can-i-claim-my-rewards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-when_can_i_claim_my_rewards">When can I claim my rewards?</span></h2>
<p>Posts and comments remain active for 7 days. When the period is over, you are able to claim their earned rewards. In your Wallet, click the Claim Rewards button to add the tokens to your account.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-the-difference-between-steem-steem-power-and-steem-dollars" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-the-difference-between-steem-steem-power-and-steem-dollars"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_the_difference_between_steem__steem_power__and_steem_dollars">What is the difference between STEEM, Steem Power, and Steem Dollars?</span></h2>
<p><strong>STEEM</strong> - STEEM is the base liquid currency token in the platform. STEEM can be powered up into Steem Power, traded for Steem Dollars, or transferred to other accounts. It is a cryptocurrency token, similar to bitcoin.</p>
<p><strong>Steem Power</strong> - Steem Power (abbreviated SP) is a measurement of how much influence a user has in the Steem network. The more Steem Power a user holds, the more they can influence the value of posts and comments. Steem Power is less liquid. If a user wishes to âPower Downâ SP, they will receive equal distributions of the STEEM weekly, over a 13 week period.</p>
<p><strong>Steem Dollars</strong> - Steem Dollars (commonly abbreviated SBD) are liquid stable-value currency tokens designed to be pegged to $1 USD. Steem Dollars can be traded with STEEM, and transferred to other accounts for commerce or exchange.  Steem Dollars may also be converted into STEEM via a process that takes 3.5 days.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-delegated-steem-power" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-delegated-steem-power"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_delegated_steem_power">What is delegated Steem Power?</span></h2>
<p>Users have the option to delegate Steem Power to other users. When a user is delegated Steem Power - their Resource Credits, content votes, and curation rewards are calculated as if it were their own Steem Power. Users are not able to power down or cash out delegated Steem Power however, as it still belongs to the original owner.</p>
<p>Most users will have a small amount of Steem Power delegated to them by the Steemit account after creating an account via steemit.com.</p>
<p>Delegated Steem Power shows up in a user's wallet below their actual Steem Power balance in parentheses.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-determines-the-price-of-steem" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-determines-the-price-of-steem"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_determines_the_price_of_steem">What determines the price of STEEM?</span></h2>
<p>The price of STEEM is based on the supply and demand of the token, as determined by buyers and sellers on the exchanges. It is similar to how the price of a commodity like gold is determined.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-i-get-more-steem-power" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-i-get-more-steem-power"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_i_get_more_steem_power">How do I get more Steem Power?</span></h2>
<p>With STEEM tokens in your wallet, click "Power Up" to turn them into Steem Power. If you have Steem Dollars, you can convert them to STEEM from your wallet, and then power up the STEEM.</p>
<p>If you donât already have STEEM or Steem Dollars in your wallet, you can purchase them using bitcoin (BTC), Ether (ETH), Litecoin (LTC), or BitShares (BTS) tokens. You may purchase BTC on various exchanges, such as Coinbase.com or Localbitcoins.com.</p>
<p>To buy:</p>
<ul>
<li>Click "Buy Steem" from the main menu in the top right corner of steemit.com, or from your wallet.</li>
<li>Select the currency to deposit, and enter the amount of that currency you wish to use.</li>
<li>Enter your Steemit account name (without the @) for "Your receive address".</li>
<li>Click the "Get Deposit Address" button.</li>
<li>Send the currency to the provided address.</li>
</ul>
<p>STEEM purchases made via steemit.com are facilitated by <a href="https://blocktrades.us" rel="nofollow">BlockTrades</a>.</p>
<p>bitcoin can also be exchanged for STEEM on external markets such as <a href="https://www.binance.com/" rel="nofollow">Binance</a>, <a href="https://www.bithumb.com/" rel="nofollow">Bithumb</a>, <a href="https://wallet.bitshares.org/" rel="nofollow">BitShares</a>, <a href="https://bittrex.com" rel="nofollow">Bittrex</a>, <a href="https://changelly.com" rel="nofollow">Changelly</a>, <a href="https://www.gobaba.com/" rel="nofollow">GOBADA</a>, <a href="https://www.gopax.co.kr" rel="nofollow">GOPAX</a>, <a href="https://hitbtc.com/" rel="nofollow">HitBTC</a>, <a href="https://www.huobi.pro/" rel="nofollow">Huobi</a>, <a href="https://www.localbitcoincash.org/" rel="nofollow">LocalBitcoinCash</a>, <a href="https://poloniex.com" rel="nofollow">Poloniex</a>, <a href="https://shapeshift.io" rel="nofollow">Shapeshift.io</a>, <a href="https://upbit.com/" rel="nofollow">UpBit</a>, and <a href="https://yensesa.com" rel="nofollow">Yensesa</a>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-long-does-it-take-steem-or-steem-power-that-i-purchased-to-show-up-in-my-account" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-long-does-it-take-steem-or-steem-power-that-i-purchased-to-show-up-in-my-account"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_long_does_it_take_steem_or_steem_power_that_i_purchased_to_show_up_in_my_account">How long does it take STEEM or Steem Power that I purchased to show up in my account?</span></h2>
<p>Transactions on the Steem blockchain typically only take about three seconds to process, but when you are purchasing the STEEM tokens using bitcoin or some other token, then the transaction must wait for the transaction to be confirmed on the other network. This can take several hours, and sometimes even days.</p>
<p>If you paid using bitcoin, the third party website <a href="https://bitcoinfees.21.co/" rel="nofollow">bitcoinfees.21.co</a> can estimate the approximate wait time of the transaction based on the fees that were paid. The third party website <a href="https://blockchain.info/" rel="nofollow">blockchain.info</a> will lookup the fees that were paid on a specific blockchain transaction.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-powering-up-and-down" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-powering-up-and-down"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_powering_up_and_down">What is powering up and down?</span></h2>
<p><strong>Powering up</strong> - If you have STEEM tokens, you can Power Up to Steem Power to get more voting influence on posts and comments. Having more Steem Power also increases the amount of curation rewards and new vested tokens that you can earn. More SP also grants more influence on approving Steem witnesses.</p>
<p><strong>Powering down</strong> - If you have Steem Power, you can power down to turn it into liquid STEEM over a period of time. The system will transfer 1/13 of your Steem Power to STEEM each week for about three months (13 weeks), starting 1 week from the time it is started. However, you will lose your influence in the network proportionally to how much is powered down, so think about it carefully. Power downs can be stopped at any time.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-do-the-dollar-amounts-for-pending-payouts-represent" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-do-the-dollar-amounts-for-pending-payouts-represent"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_do_the_dollar_amounts_for_pending_payouts_represent">What do the dollar amounts for pending payouts represent?</span></h2>
<p>The dollar amounts next to posts and comments are estimates of the potential payout that will occur when the payout period ends, based on the current voting activity and price of STEEM. These potential payout amounts may fluctuate up or down until the payout period ends.</p>
<p>Payouts occur as a combination of Steem Power and Steem Dollars. Sometimes the blockchain may substitute STEEM in place of the Steem Dollars based on market conditions.</p>
<p>The blockchain estimates the dollar value of STEEM and Steem Power based on the 3.5 day average price of STEEM reported by the witnesses. The blockchain assumes Steem Dollars are worth approximately one USD.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-will-1-steem-dollar-always-be-worth-100-usd" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#will-1-steem-dollar-always-be-worth-100-usd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-will_1_steem_dollar_always_be_worth__1_00_usd">Will 1 Steem Dollar always be worth $1.00 USD?</span></h2>
<p>The market value of a Steem Dollar is dictated by the supply and demand of the token. Therefore it is possible for 1 SBD to be worth more or less than 1 USD depending on market conditions.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-do-steem-dollar-to-steem-conversions-work" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-steem-dollar-to-steem-conversions-work"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_do_steem_dollar_to_steem_conversions_work">How do Steem Dollar to STEEM conversions work?</span></h2>
<p>If you convert Steem Dollars to STEEM, the blockchain will process the transaction over a period of 3.5 days. At the end of the 3.5 days, the SBD will be gone and replaced by approximately $1 USD worth of STEEM tokens. The "approximately 1 USD worth of STEEM tokens" is based on the median STEEM price over the 3.5 days, using the price feeds from the Steem witnesses. Depending on price fluctuations during the 3.5 days it is possible to end up with more or less than $1 USD worth of STEEM per SBD at the end of the conversion. This is an advanced user feature, and is currently only available to users using external wallets.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-is-there-a-way-for-me-to-convert-my-steem-dollars-to-steem-without-waiting-35-days" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#is-there-a-way-for-me-to-convert-my-steem-dollars-to-steem-without-waiting-35-days"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-is_there_a_way_for_me_to_convert_my_steem_dollars_to_steem_without_waiting_3_5_days">Is there a way for me to convert my Steem Dollars to STEEM without waiting 3.5 days?</span></h2>
<p>You can exchange them. Visit the internal Market, found in the main menu. There you can exchange your SBD for STEEM in real-time at whatever the current market price is.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-can-i-do-with-my-steem-tokens" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-can-i-do-with-my-steem-tokens"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_can_i_do_with_my_steem_tokens">What can I do with my STEEM tokens?</span></h2>
<ul>
<li>"Power Up" to Steem Power</li>
<li>Exchange for SBD in the internal market</li>
<li>Withdraw to an exchange, and trade for BTC or other digital tokens</li>
<li>Purchase items through third-party stores that accept STEEM tokens</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-can-i-do-with-my-sbd-tokens" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-can-i-do-with-my-sbd-tokens"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_can_i_do_with_my_sbd_tokens">What can I do with my SBD tokens?</span></h2>
<ul>
<li>Convert to STEEM via your wallet (takes 3.5 days)</li>
<li>Exchange for STEEM in the internal market</li>
<li>Withdraw to an exchange, and trade for BTC or other digital tokens</li>
<li>Purchase items through third-party stores that accept SBD tokens</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-what-is-a-mvest" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#what-is-a-mvest"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-what_is_a_mvest">What is a MVEST?</span></h2>
<p>A VEST is a unit of measurement for Steem Power. A MVEST is one million VESTS. The amount of Steem Power in one MVEST can be found on <a href="https://steemd.com/" rel="nofollow">steemd.com</a> as <code>steem_per_mvests</code>.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-can-i-sell-goods-and-services-on-steemit" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#can-i-sell-goods-and-services-on-steemit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-can_i_sell_goods_and_services_on_steemit">Can I sell goods and services on Steemit?</span></h2>
<p>Other than making a post and making sales manually, there is no interface for selling items directly on steemit.com. You can list goods and services on the third-party websites and accept payment in Steem Dollars or STEEM. You also have the option to advertise your items through Steemit posts.</p>
<p><a href="#Table_of_Contents_Economics">^</a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-how-can-i-withdraw-my-steem-or-sbd-coins" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-can-i-withdraw-my-steem-or-sbd-coins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><span id="user-content-how_can_i_withdraw_my_steem_or_sbd_coins">How can I withdraw my STEEM or SBD coins?</span></h2>
<p>STEEM and SBD tokens are readily tradable to bitcoin, which can be traded for the local currency of your choice. There is a link to "Sell" your STEEM and SBD tokens in your wallet, which uses the <a href="https://blocktrades.us/" rel="nofollow">BlockTrades</a> interface.</p>
<p>There are several guides that have been posted by users in the community for using various external exchanges to withdraw STEEM and SBD tokens. Please read the <a href="#Disclaimer">disclaimer</a> before using any of these guides to withdraw your coins. The users, guides, and exchanges listed in the guides are not endorsed by Steemit, Inc. Use the guides below at your own risk.</p>
<p>It is recommended that you withdraw a small amount first, to verify it works before withdrawing a larger amount.</p>
